MAY THLA WRITER TE LAWMMAN â‚¹9825 (Click lamah member te kan tan a ngai) Member ten kan chhiartur min ziah saktute tana kan click hmanga pawisa kan thawhkhawm chu hei le... â‚¹9825 tun thla hian kan writer te hnenah kan sem leh dawn a ni. Tun thla kan website thil vel avangin post a mumal lo deuh a, thla hmasa aiin kan hniam deuh tlat mai. Tin, a click hrim hrim pawh nikhatah click hi 1000 a awm ngai mang lo a, member lamten in mawhphurhna in hlen that ve a ngai a nia, a ziaktu lamin ziak char2 mahse a chhiartu lam intan ve si loh chuan a in balance thei miah lo a nia. kan group kal zelnan hian writer te an pawimawh tluk zetin member te pawh in pawimawh a nia... A dawng tam ber in â‚¹ 2525 a dawng a. Ziak ve hrim2 chuan Rs. 100 tal an dawng vek bawk. Tun thla chu a zawna zan 23 post tu hnenah bonus 500 kan pe a; tin, Website atanga pawimawh kan theihna tura hna pawimawh em em thawktu member te tan pawh 500 leh a nih kha, in story chhiar na tur net pack thunnan in hmang leh dawn nia... An lawmman tur hi a post tam deuh leh a chhiartu nei tam atanga siamrem a ni a, chhiartu 5000 nei chinah â‚¹50 zel a ni a, chhiartu 2500 nei chinah â‚¹ 25 zel a ni thung. Note! Writer te in vaiin Inbox lamah in dawnzat hrilh in ni a, eng emaw tih sual palh a awm chuan khawngaihin min hrilh hre dawn nia...

STORY A LINK A KAN DAHNA CHHAN. (A la hre lo leh hre tawh tan pawh) Member thar kan pun belh zel avangin engvanga website a vek story dah thin nge kan nih hre lo tam tak kan awm nual avangin i han sawi nawn leh teh ang. 1. Kan group hi story group a ni a, member zawng zawng hi story chhiar duh avanga group join vek hi kan ni a. 2. Kan group-ah hian mi pawimawh ber te chu te story writer te hi an ni. 3. Kan writer te hian story kan chhiar theihnan anmahni hun leh ngaihtuahna tam tak senga story an ziah mai piah lamah mahni neihsum sengin story post na tur net pack an thun ve a ngai thin. 4. Kan writer te hun leh ngaihtuahna chu keini pek let theih a ni hauh lo a, mahse kan pek let ve theih chhun chu an netpack man tur leh an tha hahman tlem a zawng website kal tlangin kan pe let ve thei a ni. 5. Engtin nge website hmangin kan pek let ve theih?  Hetah hian a pawimawh ber chu MEMBER te kan ni a, website-a story kan chhiar laia advertisement lo lang reng reng hi company ho rawn dah a ni a, kan mit la zawng advertisement picture kan click khan advertisement dahtu company ten website hnenah pawisa an chawi thin a, chu mi tling khawm chu writer te hnenah an netpack/pocket money atan kan sem ve leh thin a ni. KAN WRITER TE LEH WEBSITE HI in tel lo chuan kan kal thei lo a, member ten hah taka kan story chhiar tur ngaihnawm tak tak min ziah sak tu kan writer te tan advertisement click hmangin netpack kan tumsak ve thei in, a chhiartu ni ringawt lo in lawmthu sawi tu i ni vek ang u. I STORY CHHIARTUR ZIAKSAK TU CHE HNENAH LAWMTHU I SAWI NAN ADVERTISEMENT I LO CLICK THIN DAWN NIA.

STORY AWLSAM TAK A ZAWN DAN Mobile atanga story chhiar thinte tan facebook-ah search a awm ve loh avangin in story duhzawng inbox emaw post siamin in zawt fo thin a, midang zawh buai ngai lo a, mahni a awlsam taka zawn dan a awm a, hetiang hian i ti thin dawn nia. 1. Website atangin : storyfb.com ah i lut ang a, search ah khan i story chhiar duh i type ang a, website-ah a awm chuan a rawn lang mai ang. 2. Google atangin : google-ah i lut ang a, i story hming leh storyfb tih i chhu ang a, a rawn lang mai ang. Entirnan, i story chhiar duh hmiang kha 'I LOVE YOU' tih ni ta se, google-ah i love you storyfb tiin i zawng ang a, a rawn lang mai ang.
Group invite na kha lo dah leh teh uuu.

STORY A LINK A KAN DAHNA CHHAN. (A la hre lo leh hre tawh tan pawh) Member thar kan pun belh zel avangin engvanga website a vek story dah thin nge kan nih hre lo tam tak kan awm nual avangin i han sawi nawn leh teh ang. 1. Kan group hi story group a ni a, member zawng zawng hi story chhiar duh avanga group join vek hi kan ni a. 2. Kan group-ah hian mi pawimawh ber te chu te story writer te hi an ni. 3. Kan writer te hian story kan chhiar theihnan anmahni hun leh ngaihtuahna tam tak senga story an ziah mai piah lamah mahni neihsum sengin story post na tur net pack an thun ve a ngai thin. 4. Kan writer te hun leh ngaihtuahna chu keini pek let theih a ni hauh lo a, mahse kan pek let ve theih chhun chu an netpack man tur leh an tha hahman tlem a zawng website kal tlangin kan pe let ve thei a ni. 5. Engtin nge website hmangin kan pek let ve theih?  Hetah hian a pawimawh ber chu MEMBER te kan ni a, website-a story kan chhiar laia advertisement lo lang reng reng hi company ho rawn dah a ni a, kan mit la zawng advertisement picture kan click khan advertisement dahtu company ten website hnenah pawisa an chawi thin a, chu mi tling khawm chu writer te hnenah an netpack/pocket money atan kan sem ve leh thin a ni. KAN WRITER TE LEH WEBSITE HI in tel lo chuan kan kal thei lo a, member ten hah taka kan story chhiar tur ngaihnawm tak tak min ziah sak tu kan writer te tan advertisement click hmangin netpack kan tumsak ve thei in, a chhiartu ni ringawt lo in lawmthu sawi tu i ni vek ang u. I STORY CHHIARTUR ZIAKSAK TU CHE HNENAH LAWMTHU I SAWI NAN ADVERTISEMENT I LO CLICK THIN DAWN NIA.

> COMING SOON < . BASTARD . Carter Reynolds ka ni a, sÃ¢wn ka ni. Chu chu ka naupan lai atang tawh leh ka thih ni thleng pawha ka nihna tur a ni.  Eng thil mahin a thlak danglam tawh dawn lo va, hliah khuh zo turin eng thil mah hi a lian tawk hek lo. Ka nun hi ka hua a, ka nihna hian ka pawi thuk tak a sawi a ni mai lo va, thil tha dang zawng zawng pawh ka tan chuan engmah lo mai an ni. Kan thenawm nula Indi ka hmuh hma zawng kha chuan. . . A mitmeng vawikhat ka hmuhna atang khan keimahah danglam a awm nghala,  chu chu ka tan chuan thil thiang ve lo ang maiah ka ngai thung. Ka rilru ngaihtuahna ti danglam vektu tawn chu ka duh lo va, mahse chu erawh ka thlakhlelh ber a ni lawi si. . . A mitmu lian kalh, fiah leh hring mawi tak maia min han melh zet zawng, ka thlarau thleng pawha hmuh theihna thiltihtheihna a nei ta hial emaw ka ti rum rum mai. Chu chuan min ti hlauthawng a ni. Ani chu he ka hringnun thim leh chirh dum hmunah hi chuan ni eng no sur leh chhimbal zam mawi tak ang a ni a, mahse kei erawh chuan chu thil mawi tak chu ka ngaina ve hauh lo. . . ***.  ***.  *** . Ka hming chu Indiana Montgomery a ni a, kum 6 mi lek ka nih laiin ka hringtu nu in min thih sana.. Chutih rual erawh chuan hringnun nuam tak leh thian fel tak tak ka nei a. Ka pa fa neih chhun leh a khawvel ka ni a, a tan ka hlut ang bawkin ani aia hlu ka tan an awm lo. . Kan thenawm a Carter Reynolds-a te an lo awm atang chiah chuan ka nun chu a inthlak dawrh a. A hmel pa hrak mai chuan min bual Ã¢ vek a, ka suangtuahna chauha cheng tur mipa ni tur chuan ka thei kher angem? A miziaah mipa zia dik tak i hmu ang a, a mitmengah erawh natna thuk tak a nei tih i hmu thung ang.  . A mi tih dan vel chu ka huat zawng tak a ni a, mahse ka haw chuang si lo. Hahdamna leh zalenna hmuh saka, a nun thim tak laka eng chhit saktu nih ka duh. Mahse aman a tum tlat si lo. . Vawi tam tak amah hnaih lo turin min ti a, ka thei lo chu a nih hi. J Lalzahngaia > â€ŽSTORY STORY A LINK A KAN DAHNA CHHAN. (A la hre lo leh hre tawh tan pawh) Member thar kan pun belh zel avangin engvanga website a vek story dah thin nge kan nih hre lo tam tak kan awm nual avangin i han sawi nawn leh teh ang. 1. Kan group hi story group a ni a, member zawng zawng hi story chhiar duh avanga group join vek hi kan ni a. 2. Kan group-ah hian mi pawimawh ber te chu te story writer te hi an ni. 3. Kan writer te hian story kan chhiar theihnan anmahni hun leh ngaihtuahna tam tak senga story an ziah mai piah lamah mahni neihsum sengin story post na tur net pack an thun ve a ngai thin. 4. Kan writer te hun leh ngaihtuahna chu keini pek let theih a ni hauh lo a, mahse kan pek let ve theih chhun chu an netpack man tur leh an tha hahman tlem a zawng website kal tlangin kan pe let ve thei a ni. 5. Engtin nge website hmangin kan pek let ve theih?  Hetah hian a pawimawh ber chu MEMBER te kan ni a, website-a story kan chhiar laia advertisement lo lang reng reng hi company ho rawn dah a ni a, kan mit la zawng advertisement picture kan click khan advertisement dahtu company ten website hnenah pawisa an chawi thin a, chu mi tling khawm chu writer te hnenah an netpack/pocket money atan kan sem ve leh thin a ni. KAN WRITER TE LEH WEBSITE HI in tel lo chuan kan kal thei lo a, member ten hah taka kan story chhiar tur ngaihnawm tak tak min ziah sak tu kan writer te tan advertisement click hmangin netpack kan tumsak ve thei in, a chhiartu ni ringawt lo in lawmthu sawi tu i ni vek ang u. I STORY CHHIARTUR ZIAKSAK TU CHE HNENAH LAWMTHU I SAWI NAN ADVERTISEMENT I LO CLICK THIN DAWN NIA.

STORYFB.COM WHATSAPP GROUP (Member te hriattur tlem a zawng)  1. Website a mi story link kan share a nih loh chuan, story emaw thil dang hrim hrim post phal a ni lo, breaking news emaw thil pawimawh bik ang chi erawh thudang ni se.  2. Group hi 1 atanga 18 thleng siam a ni a, member awmduh kan pun dan azirin group siam belh zel tur a ni  3. Group 1 aia tamah awm phal a ni lo, group zawng zawngah link kan share a in ang vek.  4. Story kan chhiar anih chuan advertisement picture click hi kan tih ngei ngei turah i ngai theuh ang u. Hei hi he group leh website kan siam chhan a ni si a.   5. Kan thupui chu CLICK! CLICK! CLICK! CLICK! CLICK! CLICK! a ni tawp mai......
STORY AWLSAM TAK A ZAWN DAN Mobile atanga story chhiar thinte tan facebook-ah search a awm ve loh avangin in story duhzawng inbox emaw post siamin in zawt fo thin a, midang zawh buai ngai lo a, mahni a awlsam taka zawn dan a awm a, hetiang hian i ti thin dawn nia. 1. Website atangin : storyfb.com ah i lut ang a, search ah khan i story chhiar duh i type ang a, website-ah a awm chuan a rawn lang mai ang. 2. Google atangin : google-ah i lut ang a, i story hming leh storyfb tih i chhu ang a, a rawn lang mai ang. Entirnan, i story chhiar duh hmiang kha 'I LOVE YOU' tih ni ta se, google-ah i love you storyfb tiin i zawng ang a, a rawn lang mai ang.

AUGUST THLA NETPACK MAN TU TE  (Ka ziak duah zel a, chhiar peih pawh in awm leh pek lo ang) Zawhna : Story leh writer kan neih belh zel theih nan eng nge pawimawh ang? Chhanna : Kan chhanna a in ang tlangpui a, tlema zawhna ni lo deuh chhang pawh kan awm leh zeuh bawk a.... Kan chhanna tlangpui chu hetiang hi a ni a. 1. Advertisement picture click uar - advertisement kan lo click sak avang hian a chhiartute tan channa engmah a awm lo a, story min ziahsaktuten story a thlawna an post theih nan netpack kan tum sakna a ni. 2. Commment - An story kan chhiarsak ngei a ni tih leh a story kalhmanga kan ngaihdan kan sawi chhuah ve na a ni a, hei hi writer te ah thuk takin hna a thawk thin. 3. Like - Like avang hian an story kan ngaina tih an hria a, like tu neih tam hi nuam an ti thin a, an story hlawhtlin leh tlin loh teh nan an hmang ve fo thin. A pawimawh hlawm khawp mai, ka belh ve duh chu story thar ziaktute hi i chhiarsak ve thin ang u, kan chhiar chhunah an phur theihnan tawiawm an pawimawh bik a nia, zam tak leh chhiarsaktu an nei lo palh ang tih hlau ngawih ngawihin an post thin a nia. Tunah kan writer lar tak pakhat pawh hi group dangah story eng emaw zat a post tawh hnuah pawh kan group ah chhiartu a neih ve loh hlau in a post ngam lo hial a sin. Writer lar ber te zinga a kai theih phahna chhan pakhat Group danga a story lo post ho phawrh chhuaksak vang an ni lawi si... Writer thiam tak tak tur in phum ru tunah pawh hian in awm teuh ang.... Thubelh : Ka ngen duh che u chu, facebook a story ziah hi ziahna a ni lo a, hobby a ni a, hunawl remchanga ziak thin an ni a, an post hman loh emaw mihring ve tho an ni a peih loh chang te pawh an nei ang, chutih hunah chuan i nawrlui vak vak thin lo ang u, story ziah hi 'Thil nuam' ni lo a 'Phurrit' anga an ngaih chuan an ziak reng peih hauh lo ang. Tin, phur reng theih a ni lo a, an phur loh changa kan fuihna te hian a tanpui nasa thin tih kan hre reng dawn nia. Vei zawng sawi hi chuan ka tui leh lutuk thin a, min lo hrethiam teh u, Thum kan vawr a, a vannei mi 5 netpack man tu te chu.... A chhang ve hrim2 hming dah tel vek a ni e, in chhanna a dik emaw dik lo emaw lam aiin group thil tihah in tel ve hrim2 na kha kan duh ber chu a ni e... Muantei Zomi Jacob Ysreborn Chhuangtei Starla Renthlei Bethseby Lalruatpuii Ralte Ngts Khawlhring Inbox lamah in number, company, netpack/topup leh 2g/3g tih in rawn sawi dawn nia...

J Lalzahngaia > â€ŽSTORY GROUP TAN THU LUNGCHHIATTHLAK (comment theih loh in tih sup2 chhan chu a khawi lam ve ve pawh sawi chhiatna lam a awm palh ka duh loh vang a ni a, khawngaihin tu tan pawha chhiar hreawm tur chi chu i post lo ang u, comment in duh ve miau si a, comment chu hawng ila, tawngkam erawh i fimkhur hram ang u) Hun rei deuh tawh atang khan writer thenkhat anmahni hlut a enkawla buaipuitu nia ka lo inhriat ve laiin an status lamah leh post ah min bei zeuh2 tawh thin a, a mimal tin ten lungawi loh na an neih chuan siamthat tumin theih tawpin ka bei thin a, chu chuan pawngpawrhna a siam a ni mahna, ka chungah an inluling tawlh2 ni ber in a lang a. Vawiin chhun khan ka status la kawi luiin ka status lamah an rawn che deuh nual a, ka delete a ka update nawn leh hnu ah pawh an la rawn che ta zel a, an thuduhlai la-in an status lamah nen lam min cheksawlh zui a, hei hi mahni awmna group admin te tih dan tur a ni ngai lo a, a buaipuitu ber thungrulh dan tur a ni hek lo. Hetiang mi hi ka group enkawlah an awm zel ka duh lo a, anni pawhin ka enkawlna hnuai a awm hi engah teh chiam an ngai lo niin a lang. Story group atanga thil in tan a ni a, mimal thil ni lo in group thil a nih avangin group admin active taka enkawltu awmchhun ka nih tawh angin action ka la ta a ni ber. Anni pawhin sawi duh an nghah ang a, kan insawi chhawk chuan group tan hlawkna awm miah si lo in thutha aiin inhnialah kan tlak dawn tih a chiang reng a, chuvang chuan hetia tih fel mai hi a tha, an status lamah erawh ka hming a chuang ngei ang tih ka ring e. Keini tluka writer te ngaihsak leh buaipui hi group an tam bik kher lo ang, writer leh member tinte hi kan hlutin kan ngai pawimawh che u a, chutiang anih avang chuan vawi 2/3 lai chu boruak ka siamtha tawh emaw ka tih hnu ah an rawn pawng leh thin si a, hetiang reng a nih dawn chuan thawhho na tha neih theih a ni dawn si lo a tiin ui em em chungin group atangin kan writer te chu ka remove ta... An story in chan phah dawn chuang lo a, mahni puala group nei sa vek, kan group-a an awm hma atanga story ziak tawh thin an ni a, an ziak zel ang tih ka ring a, kan group tana mi thawhhlawk ber ber te an ni a, story tam tak kan group ah min post sak tawhna avangin an chungah lawmthu ka sawi bawk e. An kalzelna turah duhsakna ka hlan a, tang deuh2 tur leh midang group-ah an insuan lutte anih chuan keimah anga mi tlinglo hi an tawn tawh loh ka duhsak bawk e. (tunkin zing dar 3 chho vel a ka ziah kha a nia, boruak a tihpunlun ka hlauh avangin ka post ang nge post lo tih ka inkhap reng a, mahse member te in phawklek nasa si a, ka tih chhan hi in hriat ve ka duh avangin ka ziah ngai ang chiah2 in ka rawn post leh a ni e, hei hian boruak a tih daih ka beisei takzet a, group pawha kal ngaiin a kal zel ka beisei bawk)
Lo nh tak chu mole,in ngeih dial2a om h ahar rualin atha bok si...

A tawp nan tih in hnen a sawi a ngai mai hi pawi ka ti a, Pawi ka tih zia sawi ngaihna ka hre lo ani, thiam ka ni hauh lo va, kan thu ziah min lo chhiarsak thin vangin ka lawm em em a, thlah na engmah nei lo a awm chu  ka VVIP te in nih miau a vangin lawmthu ka sawi nawn leh ni rawh se, in lak ah ka lawm em em a, tih lungawi lo chang che u ka ngah ang, ka tih sual zawng zawng ah min ngaidam ula, min hre reng thei lo tih ka hria, mahse in tan kan tan thu ka la ziak reng dawn tih erawh min lo hriat sak ula, midang kei ni ai a ziah lam a tui leh in pe zo zawk an la rawn chhuak ngei ang, duhsak na ka hlan mawlh mawlh bawk.  Ka VVIP te min thlawp na vangin ka lawm a, in tel lo a engmah ni lo hian, bul ka han tan tha leh dawn chu a ni a,  mahse le, in awm a vang a awm ve mai hian in tan kan tan tih theih ka van nei tlem si em aw!. J Lalzahngaia > â€ŽSTORY NGAIHDAM DILNA Group writer tha ber ber te leh member te lakah ngaidam ngaiin ka awm leh ta, Keimah leh keimahin ka inhmu lian thin lutuk a, ka chapo na hian ka tih ve tlemte te kha a pawimawh ta ber emaw min tih tir a, in remna aiin buaina ah zel min hnuklut a, keimah leh keimah ka inti mualpho zawk a ni. In rilru ka tihnat na leh ka tih phawklek avangin an chunga ka tihsual apiang hnenah ngaihdam ka dil e. Group hi ka thil tih ve tlem te avangin kha a nei tu ni lo pui hian nei tu leh thu ber emaw ka lo in ti thin a, mahni thei in tih tawkna avangin group hi keimah chauhin enkawl theiah ka in ngai a, midang rawn ka tum ngai reng reng lo a, ka famkim loh teh lul nen hian engkim hria ah ka lo in ngai a ni. Ni zan hmasa ah darkar 4 vel chiah ka mu a, ka thinrim lo in up tawh nen ka puak chhuak ta thut a ni ber mai, ka inchhir ngawih ngawih a, ka zak ngawih ngawih bawk. Tunah chuan group admin ten ro an rel ang ang, ka pawm emaw pawm lo emawah an thu ang zela kal a tul zia ka hrechiang ta a, tun a chinah vawikhatmah keima mimal thu in engmah ka ti tawh ngai lo, admin ten website a post loh an rel anih pawhin lawm takin ka pawm ang a, a ngai a kal an rel anih pawhin phur takin ka theih ve na apiangah group tan ka ti zel tawh ang. Writer te pawh add leh vek an ni e, story post chungchangah pawh a duhin an duhna apiangah post rawh se, in ngirhngho na a awm ai chuan a la hlu zawk tho tho...

STREET OF HAVEN Sherrie Austin . . Lalpa duhtak, zan dang pawha rawn be ziah tu che, pindan 304 na a mi bawk kha ka ni e .  Tunah hian zing lam dar 2 a ri tawha, mahni laikhumzawlah tui taka mi zawng zawng an mut siai siai laiin kan khum kiangah erawh nunna leh thihnain hun an inchuk mek zela.  Tuna kan kianga natna avanga mu mek ka fanu duhtak hian khawvar hun min thlenpui zo angem tih pawh ka chiang ngam ta lo. Kei chuan ka mittui tla lo tura ka beih hram hram laiin ani erawh chuan a nunna tur a tan a bei mek a ni si a.  . . Hello God, it's me again. 2:00 a.m., Room 304. Visiting hours are over, time for our bedside tug of war. This sleeping child between us may not make it through the night. I'm fighting back the tears as she fights for her life. . . Lalpa, i awmna vanram kawtchhuahah khan i tlansate bakah angel tam tak i bula awm tur i nei a ni tih ka hria. Chuti chung pawh chuan engvanga ka fanu hi min la laksak duh cheu nge i nih le? Nang pawhin i hria a ni lawmni, engtik niah emaw chuan i kiangah kumkhuain a la awm dawn a ni tih hi. Tunah rih  chuan he khawvelah hian ka la mamawh ve rih a ni. . Chumai bakah hmeichhe naupang, kum 7 mi mai a la ni a, amaha tih theih pawh a la nei tha thum lo. I kianga chawl tawh turin lo hruai ta tehreng pawh ni la amah mai chuan a kal thiam lovang. Tunge vanram kawtchhuahah chuan kaiin lo hruai ang? . . Well, it must be kind of crowded, On the streets of Heaven. So tell me: what do you need her for? Don't you know one day she'll be your little girl forever. But right now I need her so much more. She's much too young to be on her own: Barely just turned seven. So who will hold her hand when she crosses the streets of Heaven? . . . Min han hrilh mah teh Lalpa, a piancham kan lawm hnuhnung ber tuma a birthday cake bati a chhem hlum laia a duhthusam a sawite kha i la hriatpui reng a ni tih hi? A len hunah chuan Sakawr chunga chuan ve ngei a la tum thu leh a puitlin hunah a pa anga mipa tha pasal neih a tum ve zia a sawi te kha. Tunah pawh tlansa tam tak i nei reng chung hian chu chu i tan ala tawk zo lo em ni? He leia ka rohlu ber leh ka la mamawh ngawih ngawih ka fanu min laksak i tum mai ni? Kum 7 a tling awrh chauh a ni a, amaha vanram kawtchhuaha rawn kal beuh beuh tur atan chuan a la te lulai emai. Tuin nge a kutah lo chelhin lo kai ang? . . Tell me God, do you remember the wishes that she made, As she blew out the candles on her last birthday cake? She wants to ride a pony when she'd big enough. She wants to marry her Daddy when she's all grown up. . . . Lalpa, i hriat ve vek kha, ka tan vantirhkoh a ni tih hi. A tan chenna hmun nuam tak i buatsaih sak ang tih pawh ka hai lo ve. Mahse tunah rih chuan kan bulah pawh ala hlim ve em em rih a, a tan theihtawp kan chhuah ve asin. Tunah hian ka tawngtaina hi i chhan ngei dawn leh dawn loh ka hre lo. Mahse i zahngaihna ka ngen tak meuh meuh a ni. Lalpa, ka rilru nat tur zia hi min dawnpui hram teh. Nang pawhin i fapa neih chhun i chan ve tawh kha. . . Lord, don't you know she's my angel You got plenty of your own And I know you hold a place for her But she's already got a home Well I don't know if you're listenin' But praying is all that's left to do So I ask you Lord have mercy, you lost a son once too . . . Mahse Lalpa, hei erawh chiang takin ka hria e. Nang chuan kan tana tha lo turin ro min rel sak ngai lova, i thuthlukna siam tawh chu eng thil mahin a sawhsawn thei tawh lo a ni tih ka hria e. Vawiinah hian a nunna i la ta a nih pawhin nang chuan kei aiin i enkawl thiam zawk dawn a, a tana tha tur pawh i hre zawk e. Mahse a la naupangin ala te si a, amaha Vanram kawtchhuah a rawn thlen hunah a kutah chelhin lo kai tlat ang che aw.... . . Lord, I know once you've made up your mind, There's no use in beggin'. So if you take her with you today, will you make sure she looks both ways, And would you hold her hand when she crosses the streets of Heaven. . . â€“Noah Hringngen

"A È›awng bul lamah chuan 'poltergeist' tih hi German thumal pahnih -'poltern' (ri siamchhuak) leh 'geist' (thlarau) aÈ›anga lo kal ani a, 'thlarau/ramhuai bengchheng' tihna anih ber chu.  A hming ang hi anih dan pawh ani ber a, mihring te tana awm tinuamlo leh hnawksak rawngkai vek an ni.  Tin, In vawm, kawngkhar leh bang tihrik, chhuat rah ri, mihring aw ri lo chhuak, a titu awm silova inchhung bungraw hrang hrang chesawn, mihring tihnat, sih leh ben te hi a hnathawh dan ber ani a. Thlahrang (ghost) nen hian ngaihfin awl tak mai ani bawk a. Mahse an hrang hlak ani.  Thlahrang (ghost) chetna chuan hmun eng emaw bik a huam a, mihring awmlohna hmun ah pawh a chet tur angin a che tho a, mihring kher a tum chuanglo.  Poltergeist erawh chuan mihring a bitum thin a, a chet rei zawng pawh hi a in anglo thluah mai, darkar reilote atanga thla eng emaw zat pawh a awh thei ani. STORY AWLSAM TAK A ZAWN DAN Mobile atanga story chhiar thinte tan facebook-ah search a awm ve loh avangin in story duhzawng inbox emaw post siamin in zawt fo thin a, midang zawh buai ngai lo a, mahni a awlsam taka zawn dan a awm a, hetiang hian i ti thin dawn nia. 1. Website atangin : storyfb.com ah i lut ang a, search ah khan i story chhiar duh i type ang a, website-ah a awm chuan a rawn lang mai ang. 2. Google atangin : google-ah i lut ang a, i story hming leh storyfb tih i chhu ang a, a rawn lang mai ang. Entirnan, i story chhiar duh hmiang kha 'I LOVE YOU' tih ni ta se, google-ah i love you storyfb tiin i zawng ang a, a rawn lang mai ang.

AUGUST THLA WRITER TE LAWMMAN â‚¹10480 (Click lamah member ten hma kan sawn e) Chhiartu lam pawh kan pun tak zel avangin Episode tin chhiartu singkhat nei tling chinin episode khatah Rs. 100 zel an dawng tawh ang. Member ten kan chhiartur min ziah saktute tana kan click hmanga pawisa kan thawhkhawm chu hei le... â‚¹10480 tun thla hian kan writer te hnenah kan sem leh dawn a ni. A click tu lam pawhin click in uar chho ve zel a, thil lawmawm tak a ni, story ngaihnawm tak tak min ziahsaktute tan story kan chhiar apiangin kan click zel dawn nia, story ngai chhiar pawhin click nawn tih a awm thei lo a nia, darkar 24 a liam tawh tawh chuan click lamah story ngai tih a awm thei lo... Advertisement a in load zawh khan back nghal lo in second 10 tal an website en sak tur a nih kha aw (Second 10 tal en kual sak hi a pawimawh lai ber tih hre nawn leh ila...) Writers 20 in an story an post a, a dawng tam ber in â‚¹ 2680 a dawng a. Ziak ve hrim2 chuan Rs. 100 kan tih thin kha click tu kan pun tak avangin tun thla atang chuan 150 an dawng vek bawk. A laklawha tawpsan hnihne a tlem zawk nan Story complete lo a chawlhsan ho reng rengin lawman an dawng lo bawk, chhiartu engzat pawh nei se an complete leh phawt loh chuan lawmman hi pek theih a ni lo.. An lawmman tur hi a post tam deuh leh a chhiartu nei tam atanga siamrem a ni a, chhiartu 5000 nei chinah â‚¹50 zel a ni a, chhiartu 2500 nei chinah â‚¹ 25 zel a ni thung. Tun thla bonus chu Haylor Sept hnenah Rs. 500 kan pe dawn a ni, Ani Doctor (MBBS) zir chungin story hi a ziak thin a, test leh project neuh neuh tih tur nei trun chungin a rawn ziak ve ngat ngat thin a, zan rei tak takah kan chhiar tur story a ziah zawhah a zirlai a zir tan thei chauh thin a, zing dar 3 thleng te a men a ngai hial thin, a taimakna leh reader te a ngaih pawimawhna hi a ropui em avangin bonus dawn hi a phu hliah hliah a ni. Tin, Website a kal zel theihna tura hna pawimawh em em thawktu member te tan pawh 500 kan dah hrang leh a, in story chhiar na tur net pack thunnan in hmang leh dawn nia... GROUP HMA LAKNA TUR  * Competition. * Mi harsate tan christmas thilpek. COMPETITION: Kum danga kan lo tih tawh thin angin kuminah pawh story la post ngai lo te tan story in ziahsak competion buatsaih leh tum a ni a, tun thla hi chu kan picnic tur vel avang hian kan buai rih deuh a, kan ti thei lo tur ah ngai ila, thla tharah chuan tih ngei kan tum ang. Story ziah chak si, ziak ve ngam chiah lo te tan bul tanna chance tha tak a ni ang, nikuma kan tih atanga story ngaihnawm tak tak nei zui ta zel te pawh kan awm a, kumin ah pawh hian thiam tak tak in rawn in lar leh ngei kan beisei. A ziak ve duh tur te chu tun atang hian in lo in buatsaih dawn nia aw, lawmman pawh kan siam leh dawn a nia... CHRISTMAS THILPEK : Hei hi kumdangah pawh ka thil chak em em thin a ni a, hmalak vak ngaihna ka hriat loh avangin tih loh in hun in min liam san zel a, kuminah chuan tih ve ngei tha in ka hria a, rilru ah chuan a thei thei in pawisa thawhkhawm a, LPS Samari Mitha ah emaw khawilai home ah emaw pek tih a awm deuh a. A theih phei chuan Christmas thawmhnaw thar leina tur nei lo zawn chhuah a pek kha ka chak ber chu a ni a. He thil hi chu keima lo tawn tawh ngei anih avangin thildang zawng aia ka chak lehzual.. hei erawh hi chu november lam daih a ngaihtuah that atan awm rih se.
